Nothing Is More Tragic Than a Dead Heart 109

— Tian Hen

The Japanese have no regard for China. Even less regard for the League of Nations. They actually established the puppet state of Manchuria while the League of Nations investigation team was on its way to China. What they once hesitated and lingered over, not daring to put into practice, is now being carried out one by one. For example, the customs duties of the three northeastern provinces. Didn't the Japanese intend to seize them for a long time, but didn't dare to implement it for a long time? Now they are openly expelling customs officials and forcibly taking over. And Mr. Wang Guangming once told the people that if the puppet state were declared established, the national government would definitely order its suppression. Who would have thought that before the blood on his lips was dry, he had already gone back on his word. The great Northeast has been allowed to fall into enemy hands. Is it not heartbreaking? Furthermore. The world only has governments that lose their country, not people who lose their country. How can our people be an exception? But who knew it would be otherwise. Recently, I read the Binjiang Times, a major newspaper in Jilin Province. After the incident, it still publishes two and a half large sheets daily. What is published in it is often extremely absurd. Although it is said that they are not free under the violence of the Japanese, when writing, they might as well avoid the important and take the light, or only record the facts, or rather not write anything. They must not take the puppet state of Manchuria as the subject before writing, regard themselves as people of the puppet state of Manchuria, and openly despise the motherland, fawning on the Japanese and their Chinese lackeys. For example, when writing about Zang Shiyi, it is enough to say Zang Shiyi. Why must it be written as Governor Zang? The Japanese will never pay attention to this, saying that they cannot directly call him by his name. For example, if it is recorded that Bao Guancheng is ill, it is enough to say that Bao Guandeng is ill. But the newspaper says that Mayor Bao's government affairs are unwell. It is inevitable that people will feel nauseous for three days. It is even more hateful that the guerrillas are generally referred to as bandits and the Japanese army is praised. As the saying goes, (Nothing is more tragic than a dead heart). There is no doubt that these journalists are already dead-hearted. And the intellectual circles in the Northeast are still so shameless. Not to mention the ordinary people. This is why we feel even more heartbroken that the government is willing to lose the Northeast. Moreover, the masthead of the newspaper prominently states the first year of Datong. The Yingkou Commercial Daily has become even more intensified. In addition to the first year of Datong, there is also the Japanese Showa era. I wonder if there is still China in the hearts of these people? Or do they regard all of China as a country that has already fallen? Alas. It's extremely heartbreaking.

The Shanghai War and Weapons (8) 110

— Yi Zang

Projectiles: Projectiles vary depending on the type of guns and cannons. Gun bullets have been described above. Now, let's briefly talk about cannon shells. Among cannon shells, field gun shells include: high-explosive shells, shrapnel shells, incendiary shells, armor-piercing shells, smoke shells, illuminating shells, gas shells, signal shells, etc. Each type of shell has a special effect. Some are used to destroy buildings, some are used to suffocate and slaughter humans and animals, and some are used to burn and poison distant positions. Generally, they are used according to the situation during combat. In addition, these projectiles are loaded with fuses that ignite and explode at the desired location and time. These fuses are also divided into instantaneous fuses, short-delay fuses, anti-aircraft fuses, and igniter fuses. Recently, to reduce air pressure in igniter fuses and improve the uneven combustion power of gunpowder, timing and electricity have been used to invent mechanical fuses and electric fuses. Furthermore, to connect the fuse and the projectile, special projectiles have been created. The idea is that when the projectile reaches a certain location, the fuse's action can ignite a portion of the special bomb installed at the bottom. This is used to spray gas. The reaction force can propel it to a great distance. This type of projectile is called a Rocket-applied shell. There are many other types, such as grape shot, chain shot, iron cylinder shot, sulfur shot, etc., too numerous to mention. Depending on the shape of the various guns and cannons and the effect of the firing, the external shape and internal structure vary accordingly. This time, the Japanese army used mostly high-explosive and incendiary shells in Zhabei. The ones dropped from the air were incendiary and armor-piercing bombs. The weight of the bombs was over two thousand kilograms and under three thousand kilograms. The ones used during the Wusong landing were smoke shells. According to eyewitnesses of this newspaper, judging from the shell casings picked up in the rubble piles in Jiangwan, Wusong, and Zhabei, the larger ones reached three hundred pounds. This is enough to prove the magnitude of the damage this time.

Suspicion (Part 2) 111

— Cheng Zhanlu

Why doesn't the short man speak? The passengers in the cabin already understand clearly: he can't speak; he must be a spy, he must be a foreign-made short man. This is the unquestioned answer in everyone's mind. So, the fire of patriotism blazes! A spy has infiltrated the ship. This is intolerable; he must be caught. If we want to report him, we must secretly notify the military police and have him detained.

One by one, they whispered to each other, using the method of ants conveying messages. Before long, the whole ship knew about it. The ship arrived at ×× Town, which it usually doesn't stop at. The captain announced that the engine needed repairs and the ship and tugboat stopped one by one.

A squad of water police, acting on orders, boarded the ship to inspect. First, four machine guns were aimed at the short man who was the focus of everyone's attention, ordering him to go ashore for inspection.

The short man calmly went ashore for inspection. The water police stripped off the short man's overcoat, and the truth came out. Inside were badges and symbols, clearly indicating that he was a propaganda officer of the ××× army. There were also official documents in his pocket. He was not a spy, nor was he a foreign-made short man. He was just a military figure going to Shanghai on official business.

The silent short man also spoke at this time. Listening to his speech, it was pure Cantonese, which further proved that he was indeed a domestically produced short man, not a foreign-made short man. When the water police asked him why he was silent while sitting in the cabin, causing people to suspect him? He pointed to the plaster on his right cheek, stating that he was suffering from a toothache and was reluctant to talk to people. Furthermore, he was from Guangdong, and most of the passengers on the ship were from Jiangsu and Shanghai. They asked him in their local dialects, which he couldn't understand very well, so he could only nod in response to these kinds of expressions.

The water police apologized to the short man and also investigated the person who reported him, saying that he should not have made something out of nothing and reported it as a serious matter, causing this misunderstanding.

The person who reported it couldn't help but turn pale with fright. According to the law of retaliatory punishment for false accusations, he would have to endure a lawsuit. The water police refused to let him go and insisted on taking him to the authorities. Instead, this domestically produced short man pleaded with the water police on behalf of the person who reported him:

"He did not intentionally slander me. I really had reasons that could make people suspicious. The fault lies entirely with my toothache. I have no complaints against the person who reported me and instead express my full admiration. If everyone were as attentive to reporting spies as the people on this ship, then the enemy's spies would definitely not dare to penetrate deep into the interior as if they were in no man's land. Although I have suffered some trouble, I have endless joy, rejoicing that people's hearts are not dead and that everyone can fulfill their duty to detect spies. I've said too much. My toothache is acting up again. Let's go ashore."

With a blast of the steam whistle, the small steamer moved forward again. The suspicion just now had long since vanished. The cabin was filled with a harmonious atmosphere. There was no more whispering or private discussions. Those who had given the short man dirty looks just now were now smiling at him.

Local Supplement

Essays

On Saving the Nation Through Dancing 112

— Jin

(The investigation team will hold a grand ball tonight at 9:30 PM at the Beijing Hotel. Zhang Xueliang, Yu Fengzhi, Madame Wellington Koo, Mr. and Mrs. Shen Nengyi, and other Chinese and foreign dignitaries will attend.)

Yesterday, this newspaper's dispatch from Beiping had such a message. At the time, after reading this piece of news, I couldn't help but applaud and rejoice wildly.

Mr. Zhang Xueliang has always been generous and magnanimous. Apart from not avenging the murder of his father, he also casually dismisses the hatred of national and family destruction, not caring about it. He also loves peace and has always adhered to the policy of non-resistance. Therefore, Japan was able to safely and completely occupy all of the three northeastern provinces in a matter of days. Mr. Zhang Xueliang's attitude (treating hatred and favor equally) cannot but be deeply admired by anyone. Mr. Zhang Xueliang also has a well-known specialty: he is a (dancing expert). He is now a member of the Central Executive Committee. One could also say that he is a (dancing committee member). Such a title on his head can be said to be truly well-deserved.

I remember that when the September 18th Incident occurred in the Northeast last year, there was a great uproar in Beiping, but Zhang Xueliang could not be found. Later, he was found in a certain aristocratic ballroom, where he was holding a dance partner and performing his specialty, stepping to the rhythm of the "waltz" in the soft red and green electric lights. So some rash elements who didn't understand the ways of the world cursed him for (dancing away the nation). I say no. Even if Zhang Weilang didn't dance, how could he prevent his country from being destroyed? Dancing has wonderful uses after all.

(Saving the nation through dancing) is originally the newest and most fashionable term, but I never believed that dancing could save the nation. Who knew that when the League of Nations investigation team went to Japan the other day, the Japanese government welcomed them sincerely. Today they held a grand banquet, tomorrow they held a dance. Noble women each held wreaths, offering them diligently. This (gentle) diplomacy is truly breathtaking and unprecedented. Therefore, the investigation team could not refuse the Japanese government's hospitality and stayed in Japan for about two weeks. I laughed at my own dullness. The meaning of saving the nation through dancing has such a wonderful effect. Now that the investigation team has arrived in Beiping, Mr. Zhang Xueliang will naturally fulfill his duty as host and entertain them diligently, needless to say, because the investigation team's inspection is extremely important to the Dong Province issue. This time, the investigation team held a grand ball at the Beijing Hotel. This conference seems to be dominated by the investigation team in name, with Zhang Xueliang as the guest. However, Zhang Xueliang had such a banquet before, and then the investigation team also held a grand conference to respond with elegance. There is no doubt. Therefore, I think of our country's diplomacy. Other means are far inferior to Japan. Only dancing diplomacy is indeed Zhang Xueliang's specialty. The way to save the nation may lie in this. Therefore, people say that Zhang Xueliang lost the nation through dancing. I can only say that Zhang Xueliang can save the nation through dancing.

Popular Literature and Art

The Tale of the Difficult Chicken 113

Chen'er lived on North Sichuan Road in Shanghai, less than half a mile from the former Japanese military headquarters. During the January 28th Incident this year, he fled in a panic, unable to take anything with him. At that time, there were two roosters in his residence. Before leaving, he locked them in a corner of the house, feeding them leftover grains, which were hardly enough to last them for three days. By the beginning of March, our army, in accordance with the League of Nations' resolution, withdrew its troops. Chen'er went to check on his residence after seven days. The destruction in the places he passed by was indescribable. Few of the neighboring residences were intact, but Chen'er's residence was unharmed. When he went upstairs, he suddenly heard a sound coming from the corner of the room. He quickly looked at it, thinking that even the chicken could not survive, but he still hoped that one of them would. Counting the days, it had been thirty-eight days. How amazing this chicken is! It had escaped slaughter and the flames of war, relying on a small amount of food to barely survive. As soon as it heard a human voice, it crowed. Did it know what was happening, or did it not know? Moreover, the area was so close to the war zone, and countless houses were destroyed by artillery fire. Yet Chen'er's residence was the only one spared. Perhaps it was due to the chicken's ability to endure hunger and hardship. Chen'er took it home, built a separate coop for it, intending to let it live out its days. I laughed and said, "This chicken can be called the 'difficult chicken'. We must write a tale about it." So I wrote this in the spring of the twenty-first year of the Republic of China, March. [No reward requested]

The Song of the Difficult Chicken 114

— Wei Youfang

Alas! O Chicken, come before me and let me speak to you. Why did you not urge the youth to dance in the middle of the night when the clouds of war first gathered? Why did you silently crouch before the window? Having experienced the fires of war for forty days, it must have been hard for you to survive alone in the dangerous building. I heard you had a companion, but where is it now? Could it be that it wished to learn from Zuo Botao, sharing its food with you and entering the tree? Or perhaps it was defeated in a fight for you, and you relied on the golden spurs of the Hou Sun chicken. After surviving the great disaster, fortune is at hand. Yesterday I heard that your master has renovated his house. He will raise you and let you live out your days. Your master is benevolent, and you are blessed.

Reading Chen Jun Qianfu's Tale of the Difficult Chicken 115

— Hong Foshi

Fish in a pot and swallows under the eaves weep in confusion. With its spurs still intact, it escapes the enemy's atmosphere. In a Buddhist land, frightened pigeons sometimes remain. The uncivilized people are fortunately not dead, fleeing in alarm like deer. The survival of one thing is related to the mysterious number. Thousands of families sing and weep, complaining about the skinhead army. I, an old man, still get up and dance when I hear the sound. I wish to follow the flying general and plan a miraculous feat.

Casual Chats

Ningbo People and Jiangbei People 116

— Wu

Ningbo Person: You Jiangbei people are all low-class trash. Look, in Shanghai, the people who empty chamber pots and pull rickshaws are mostly you Jiangbei people. And the most kidnappers are also Jiangbei people.

Jiangbei Person: Bullshit! You Ningbo people are the low-class ones. We empty chamber pots and pull rickshaws, but that's (self-reliance), doing things for the Chinese. But what about you Ningbo people? Hmph, doing the bidding of foreigners, being compradors, kissing the asses of (high-nosed) foreigners, being running dogs for foreigners, that's truly low-class and shameless!

Ningbo Person: Don't you kiss the asses of foreigners? You're dogs of the Japanese, doing traitorous things, killing people and setting fires. Aren't those you Jiangbei people?

Jiangbei Person: True enough, we're traitors, but (Japanese tortoises) give money! You bidding of foreigners, usually all fancy in your Western suits, won't even give us an extra copper for pulling your rickshaws, and even try to exploit us in every way. You even sold Japanese goods while boycotting them! How do you explain that? Some Jiangbei people do traitorous things because you force them to!

Ningbo Person: Who told you you can't earn money? Who told you to be poor? Poor people deserve to starve to death! You're still talking as if you're justified, how shameless!

Jiangbei Person: Ah, that's right. You have money, so you don't dare fight the Japanese. So you try every way to sell out the country. From whatever committee chairman to the bankers, there's no one who doesn't advocate compromise with those short devils. Isn't our defeat in this war all your fellow townsmen's doing?

Ningbo Person: Alright, let's not talk about that for now. But our fellow townsmen have the ability to sell out the country. Do you?

Jiangbei Person: Hahaha! So that's how it is, then (everyone can sell the country). It's not surprising that Jiangbei people do traitorous things because they're poor. Besides, those who do traitorous things are just a few minorities. Surely not every Jiangbei person is.

Ningbo Person: That's good, then. Even though I'm a Ningbo person, I don't sell out the country.

Jiangbei Person: That's right. Even though the Japanese government is imperialist, most of the Japanese people aren't bad. What else is there to say? Hahaha!

East, West, South, North

The Home of an Important Person 117

— Fushi

Spring is balmy, the tips of branches and blades of grass are full of life! Spring also sneaks through the seams of Mr. C's home.

Mr. C, reclining on the sofa, winks and assigns the evening's tasks, such as finding out about land prices in Zhabei and Jiangwan, bowing his back to rush to the banquet held by XXX at the Licha Hotel, and visiting the consul of X country with a peaceful face ::::. After thinking for a while, he felt that he couldn't handle it all. So he moved the time for meeting with a certain important person to resolve national affairs to the second evening. When he smiled with his tense, fleshy black face, he was also thinking, even if the second evening is again filled with busy affairs, there is still the third evening!::::.

Apart from the faint sound of the Fourth Concubine cracking melon seeds, the study was as silent as a tomb. Because the eldest son had gone to XXX Bank to remit money! The second son had gone to the tea dance party at XXX Dance Hall! The third daughter, fourth daughter, second concubine, and third concubine had gone to the cinema or their favorite local places. Later, the Fourth Concubine, hearing the faint flute outside the window, turned on the recording of "The Secret History of the Xuan Palace"! One, to cover up the sound of the flute outside the window and her own rapid breathing! Two, to urge him to leave quickly. Madam C, an elderly woman, had not been in charge of their petty accounts for years. Now that they (he) had all left smelling sweet, she gathered the ladies from next door around the Guangdong rosewood table to play mahjong.

The second round of frenzied flute playing and the crackling sound of mahjong tiles echoed each other outside the window. The moon goddess of the spring night also sketched her face and smiled secretly in front of the window.
